“Good evening, and if the current trends hold, this will be a triumphant night for President Mario Cuomo…”

You sit on your couch in the Governor’s mansion, watching the election night coverage. An image of Pete Wilson’s grinning mug is displayed on one side, President Cuomo on the other, and the results… well, they’re about what all the pundits expected. Tom Brokaw called the election early in the night, and the map shows it wasn’t particularly close. Wilson never really had a chance; it was just too steep a mountain to climb. Your wife walks into the room and puts a gentle hand on your shoulder. She asks if you’re okay. You stay silent at first. At the time, quitting the race seemed like the right thing to do. But after watching for months as Wilson made misstep after misstep, after seeing him fail to pounce on Cuomo’s weaknesses and fail to unite the party, you couldn’t help but think to yourself, “I could’ve done that. I would’ve done this differently. I would’ve won.” And that’s what hurts the most. Maybe you could’ve. Maybe you should’ve. Maybe you made the biggest mistake of your life when you ended your campaign. Or maybe you saved yourself from sharing the same fate as what you’re seeing unfold now. Maybe… maybe this was just how it was always meant to be.

So how can you respond to a question like, “are you okay?” You’re obviously disappointed that the GOP has lost, knowing that it almost certainly means a more conservative candidate in four years’ time. As for Wilson… well, with how opportunistic he was, he sort of had it coming, didn’t he? You exhale softly as you place your hand over Susan’s and assure her that you’re fine. And you are. Whatever else you feel — disappointment, regret, sadness — you’re fortunate to be where you are, and you’re going to keep using your platform to share your vision for America. You’ll be just a footnote in this election, a sentence or two at most in the history books, but maybe someday, someone will carry on your legacy. The rest, Governor, is up to you. Good luck and Godspeed.

} else { i++; } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { if (typeof str !== 'string' || str.indexOf('mytooltip') !== -1) { return str; } const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]); } else if (obj[key] && typeof obj[key] === 'object') { applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]); } } } applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.candidate_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json);
